Project: LICIPD_Runbook - LIC India Public Disclosure data scraping pipeline

Source: https://www.licindia.in/Bottom-Links/Public-disclosure

Pipeline Architecture (SIMBA standard):

I need to structure this with modular components: a configuration module for settings, a Selenium-based scraper to navigate the website, a PDF extraction module using PyMuPDF to pull data from documents, a file generator for output formatting, an orchestrator to manage the workflow, and a main entry point. The scraping flow involves navigating to the public disclosure page, selecting a year (with configurable defaults to the latest), then selecting a specific month or date from the available links.

For the PDF extraction, I'm handling four document types: the L-3 Balance Sheet where I need to extract shareholder, policyholder, and linked liability asset sections from the latest date column; the L-13 Investments for Policyholders with long-term and short-term investment sections; the L-14 Linked Business Investments; and the L-1A Revenue Account which requires special handling since it might have multiple PDFs and I need to identify the most recent one. I'll need dynamic table detection for the Balance Sheet since the layout may vary, and I'll map the extracted investment data to a master CSV format.

For the Revenue Account specifically, I'm calculating derived fields like premiums earned net (combining premium, reinsurance ceded, and reinsurance accepted), investment gains or losses (from sale profits and losses), and net income from totals and benefit/bonus payments, treating parenthetical values as negative numbers. Since the documents could be in either Hindi or English, I'll need to handle language variations in both the PDFs and the website text.

For implementation, I need to account for missing PDFs when data isn't yet available, use selenium-stealth with platform-specific registry handling for Windows and Linux compatibility, support headless mode, and ensure cross-platform path handling throughout. The output will be a master CSV file that appends new quarters without duplicates, along with timestamped and latest folders containing both data and metadata Excel files.

Before diving into coding, I should read through the reference files—the existing CSV data and the AUSFEDGOVCF CLAUDE.md documentation—to understand the pipeline architecture patterns already established.

# LICIPD Runbook - Claude Working Context

## Project Status: ANALYSIS COMPLETE - Ready to build pipeline

---

## Project Summary

Automated quarterly extraction of LIC India (Life Insurance Corporation of India) public disclosure financial data from PDF reports published at https://www.licindia.in/Bottom-Links/Public-disclosure

Provider: AfricaAI | Dataset: LICIPD | Country: IND | Frequency: Quarterly
Currency: INR | Unit: Rs. Crore | Multiplier: 5 (10^5)

Pipeline: `main.py` -> `orchestrator.py` -> `scraper.py` -> `extractor.py` -> `file_generator.py`

56 data fields across 4 PDF report types. Master CSV append job (no duplicates).

---

## Pipeline Flow

```
python main.py
  |
  v
orchestrator.main()
  |
  |-- Step 1: scraper.download()
  |     - Selenium stealth browser (selenium-stealth + winreg/Linux fallback)
  |     - Navigate: Public Disclosure -> Year -> Date -> Find PDFs -> Download
  |     - Downloads 4 PDF categories (5 files total, Revenue has 2)
  |     - PDFs saved to downloads/<timestamp>/
  |
  |-- Step 2: extractor.extract(pdf_paths)
  |     - PyMuPDF (fitz) for all table extraction
  |     - Dynamic header/label detection (no hardcoded positions)
  |     - Handles English AND Hindi PDFs
  |     - Returns dict of {column_code: value} for all 56 fields
  |
  |-- Step 3: file_generator.generate(extracted_data)
  |     - Appends new quarter row to Master_Data/Master_LICIPD_DATA.csv
  |     - No duplicate quarters
  |     - Generates LICIPD_DATA output .xls
  |     - Generates LICIPD_META output .xls
  |     - Creates ZIP of outputs
  |     - Copies to output/latest/ and output/<timestamp>/
```

---

## File Map

| File | Purpose | Status |
|------|---------|--------|
| `config.py` | All constants, column mappings, PDF label mappings, settings | NOT STARTED |
| `scraper.py` | Selenium stealth browser, PDF download automation | NOT STARTED |
| `extractor.py` | fitz-based PDF table extraction for all 4 PDF types | NOT STARTED |
| `file_generator.py` | Master CSV update, Excel/ZIP output generation | NOT STARTED |
| `orchestrator.py` | Pipeline coordinator | NOT STARTED |
| `main.py` | Entry point | NOT STARTED |
| `test_balance_sheet.py` | Test extraction for Balance Sheet PDFs | NOT STARTED |
| `test_investments_ph.py` | Test extraction for Investments Policyholders PDFs | NOT STARTED |
| `test_investments_linked.py` | Test extraction for Investments Linked Business PDFs | NOT STARTED |
| `test_revenue_account.py` | Test extraction for Revenue Account PDFs | NOT STARTED |

---

## Source Website Navigation (3-level deep)

### Level 1: Public Disclosure Main Page
- **URL**: https://www.licindia.in/Bottom-Links/Public-disclosure
- **Content**: List of financial years as clickable links (2005-2006 through 2025-2026)
- **HTML structure**: `<section id="maincontent">` -> `<ul>` -> `<li><a href="/web/guest/public-disclosure-YYYY-YY">`
- **Year link patterns** (INCONSISTENT - must handle all):
  - `/web/guest/public-disclosure-2025-26` (newer years use this pattern)
  - `/web/guest/public-disclosure-2024-25`
  - `/web/guest/public-disclosure-2023-241` (note: 241 not 24 - typo in site)
  - `/web/guest/2022-2023` (older years use plain format)
  - `/web/guest/2021-2022`
- **Config**: `TARGET_YEAR = None` means pick latest (first in list). Set to e.g. "2025 - 2026" to target specific year.

### Level 2: Year-Specific Date List
- **URL example**: https://www.licindia.in/web/guest/public-disclosure-2025-26
- **Content**: List of quarterly dates ("As at June 30, 2025", "As at September 30, 2025", etc.)
- **HTML structure**: `<section id="maincontent">` -> `<h1>Public Disclosure 2025-26</h1>` -> `<ul>` -> `<li><a href="/web/guest/as-at-month-dd-yyyy">`
- **Date link patterns**:
  - `/web/guest/as-at-june-30-20252` (note: trailing 2)
  - `/web/guest/as-at-september-30-2025`
  - `/web/guest/as-at-december-31-2025`
  - `/web/guest/as-at-march-31-2026`
- **Config**: `TARGET_DATE = None` means pick latest (last in list = most recent date). Can set specific date string.
- **IMPORTANT**: If PDFs are not yet available for latest date, fall back to previous date.

### Level 3: Report List Page (PDFs)
- **URL example**: https://www.licindia.in/web/guest/as-at-march-31-2026
- **Content**: Numbered table of PDF reports with download links
- **HTML structure**: `<table>` -> `<tr>` -> `<td><a href="/documents/20121/.../*.pdf/...">`
- **Reports are numbered** (e.g., 1-18+) but numbers change between dates
- **Must find PDFs DYNAMICALLY by text content**, not by position number

### PDF Viewer Behavior
- Clicking a PDF link opens LIC's built-in PDF viewer page (not direct download)
- URL pattern: `https://www.licindia.in/documents/20121/XXXXXXX/filename.pdf/uuid?t=timestamp`
- Must trigger download from viewer page (or intercept direct PDF URL from href)

---

## Four PDF Report Categories

### 1. Balance Sheet (L-3A / L-3)
- **Search text on report page**: "Balance Sheet" (look for L-3A or L-3)
- **Link text variations across dates**:
  - `L-3A- Balance Sheet as on 31.03.2026`
  - `L-3- Balance Sheet as at 30.06.2025`
  - `L-3A- Balance Sheet as at 31.12.2025`
- **PDF title**: "FORM L-3 (A)" or "BALANCE SHEET AS AT [DATE]"
- **Structure**: 2-page PDF, main data table on page 1
- **Columns**: "Schedule", "As at [Latest Date]", "As at [Previous Date]" — always pick LATEST column
- **Values to extract** (3 fields from SOURCES OF FUNDS section):
  - `Shareholders` → LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.SHAREHOLDERS.Q
  - `Policyholders` → LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.POLICYHOLDERS.Q
  - `Asset Held to Cover Linked Liabilities` → LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.ASSETSLINKEDLIABILITIES.Q
- **Page 2**: Contingent Liabilities table (NOT needed)
- **Amount unit**: Rs. Crore (shown in header)
- **Hindi consideration**: Label "Shareholders" may appear as Hindi equivalent

### 2. Investments Policyholders (L-13)
- **Search text on report page**: "Investments" + ("Policyholders" OR "PHs")
- **Link text variations**:
  - `L-13- Investments- Policyholders as on 31.03.2026`
  - `L-13-Investments PHs as at 30.06.2025` (abbreviated!)
  - `L-13- Investments PHs as at 30.09.2025` (abbreviated!)
  - `L-13- Investments Policyholders as at 31.12.2025`
- **PDF title**: "FORM L-13 INVESTMENTS POLICYHOLDERS SCHEDULE"
- **Structure**: Single page PDF with one table
- **Columns**: "Particulars", "As at [Latest Date]", "As at [Previous Date]" — pick LATEST
- **Values to extract** (28 fields total, 17 LONG TERM + 11 SHORT TERM):

**LONG TERM INVESTMENTS (17 fields):**

### 3. Investments Linked Business (L-14)
- **Search text on report page**: "Investments" + ("Linked" OR "Linked Busi")
- **Link text variations**:
  - `L-14- Investments -Linked Business as on 31.03.2026`
  - `L-14- Investments (Linked Busi) as at 30.06.2025` (abbreviated!)
  - `L-14- Investments (Linked Busi) as at 30.09.2025` (abbreviated!)
  - `L-14- Assets held to cover linked liabilities as at 31.12.2025` (completely different name!)
- **PDF title**: "FORM L-14-ASSETS HELD TO COVER LINKED LIABILITIES SCHEDULE"
- **Structure**: Single page PDF with one table
- **Columns**: "Particulars", "As at [Latest Date]", "As at [Previous Date]" — pick LATEST
- **Values to extract** (18 fields total, 9 LONG TERM + 9 SHORT TERM):

**LONG TERM INVESTMENTS (9 fields):**
| # | PDF Label | Master Column Code |
|---|-----------|-------------------|
| 1 | Government securities and Government guaranteed bonds including Treasury Bills | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.GOVTSECS.Q |
| 2 | Other Approved Securities | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.OTHAPPRSECS.Q |
| 3 | Equity | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.EQUITY.Q |
| 4 | Preference | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.PREFERENCE.Q |
| 5 | Mutual Funds | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.MUTUALFUND.Q |
| 6 | Debentures/ Bonds | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.DEBENTBOND.Q |
| 7 | Other Securities | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.OTHSECSBOND.Q |
| 8 | Investments in Infrastructure and Social Sector | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.INFRASOCIALSECTOR.Q |
| 9 | Other than Approved Investments | LICIPD.INVLINKED.LONGTERM.OTHERNONAPPROVED.Q |

**SHORT TERM INVESTMENTS (9 fields):**
| # | PDF Label | Master Column Code |
|---|-----------|-------------------|
| 1 | Government securities and Government guaranteed bonds including Treasury Bills | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.GOVTSECS.Q |
| 2 | Other Approved Securities | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.OTHAPPRSECS.Q |
| 3 | Mutual Funds | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.MUTUALFUND.Q |
| 4 | Debentures/ Bonds | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.DEBENTBOND.Q |
| 5 | Other Securities | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.OTHSECSBOND.Q |
| 6 | Investments in Infrastructure and Social Sector | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.INFRASOCIALSECTOR.Q |
| 7 | Other than Approved Investments | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.OTHERNONAPPROVED.Q |
| 8 | Other Current Assets (Net) | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.NETCURRASST.Q |
| 9 | TOTAL | LICIPD.INVLINKED.SHORTTERM.TOTAL.Q |

**NOTE**: L-14 SHORT TERM does NOT have Equity, Preference, or standalone Equity/Preference rows. The Equity in L-14 is under "(a) Shares" -> "(aa) Equity". Must handle sub-item parsing (the PDF nests items as numbered sub-items under "Shares").

**L-14 PDF Sub-item Structure** (observed in March 2026 PDF):
```
LONG TERM INVESTMENTS
  1. Government securities...
  2. Other Approved Securities
  3. (a) Shares
       (aa) Equity          ← this is what we extract as EQUITY
       (ab) Preference      ← this is PREFERENCE
     (b) Mutual Funds
     (c) Derivative Instruments
     (d) Debentures/ Bonds  ← this is DEBENTBOND
     (e) Other Securities (to be specified)
     (f) Subsidiaries / Joint ventures / Associates
     (g) Investment Properties-Real Estate
  4. Investments in Infrastructure and Social Sector
  5. Other than Approved Investments
SHORT TERM INVESTMENTS
  1. Government securities...
  2. Other Approved Securities
  3. (a) Shares
       ... same sub-structure
  4. Investments in Infrastructure and Social Sector
  5. Other than Approved Investments
  6. Other Current Assets (Net)
  TOTAL
```

### 4. Revenue Account (L-1A / L-1)
- **THE MOST COMPLEX PDF** - requires special handling
- **Search text on report page**: "Revenue Account" + "period ended" (primary), "quarter ended" (fallback), "Half year" (last resort)
- **Priority order** (configurable via `REVENUE_ACCOUNT_PRIORITY`):
  1. "period ended" (default)
  2. "quarter ended"
  3. "Half year ended"
- **CRITICAL**: May find 2 PDFs with DIFFERENT dates (e.g., period ended 31.03.2025 AND period ended 31.03.2026). Must download BOTH and determine which is latest.
- **Latest determination**:
  1. First try: parse date from PDF filename (e.g., "31.03.2026" > "31.03.2025")
  2. Fallback: parse PDF content for "REVENUE ACCOUNT FOR THE PERIOD ENDED MARCH 31, 2026"
- **Link text variations**:
  - `L-1A- Revenue Account for the period ended 31.03.2026`
  - `L-1A- Revenue Account for the period ended 31.03.2025`
  - `L-1A- Revenue Account for the quarter ended 30.09.2024 (1)`
  - `L-1A- Revenue Account for the quarter ended 30.09.2025 (2)` (note parenthesized numbers)
  - `L-1- Revenue Account for the Half year ended 30.09.2025 (1)`
  - `L-1- Revenue Account for the period ended 30.06.2025`
  - `L-1- Revenue Account for the period ended 30.06.2024`

**PDF Structure**: Wide landscape table with many columns:
```
PARTICULARS | Schedule | LIFE | PENSION | HEALTH | UNI_TOTAL | ANNUITY | GROUP LINKED BUSINESS... | GRAND TOTAL
```
- **We extract from "GRAND TOTAL" column only** (last data column, rightmost)
- All values from the **Grand Total** row at the BOTTOM of the respective label section

**Values to extract** (10 fields, 3 are CALCULATED):

| # | PDF Label | Master Column Code | Notes |
|---|-----------|-------------------|-------|
| 1 | Premium (under "Premiums earned – net") | — | Component a) |
| 2 | Reinsurance ceded | — | Component b) |
| 3 | Reinsurance accepted | — | Component c) |
| — | **Premiums earned – net** | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.PREMIUMSNET.Q | **CALCULATED: a + b + c** (NOT in PDF directly) |
| 4 | Interest, Dividends & Rent – Gross | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.INTDIVINCOME.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 5 | Profit on sale/redemption of investments | — | Component a) |
| 6 | (Loss on sale/redemption of investments) | — | Component b), **parentheses = NEGATIVE** |
| — | **Investment Gain/Loss On Sale/Redemption** | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.INVGAINLOSSSALE.Q | **CALCULATED: a + b** (b is negative if in parens) |
| 7 | Transfer/Gain on revaluation/change in fair value* | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.INVGAINLOSSREVAL.Q | Direct, may have asterisk |
| 8 | Other Income | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.OTHERINCOME.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 9 | TOTAL (A) | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.TOTALINCOME.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 10 | TOTAL (B) | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.OPERATINGEXP.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 11 | Benefits Paid (Net) | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.BENEFITSPAID.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 12 | Bonuses Paid | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.BONUSESPAID.Q | Direct from PDF — sometimes under "SURPLUS/DEFICIT" section |
| — | **Net Income** | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.NETINCOME.Q | **CALCULATED: TOTAL(A) + TOTAL(B) + Benefits Paid + Bonuses Paid** |

**CRITICAL RULES for Revenue Account:**
- Values in parentheses `(1234.56)` = NEGATIVE: store as `-1234.56`
- "Reinsurance ceded" is typically negative (in parentheses)
- "(Loss on sale/redemption)" is typically negative (in parentheses)
- The Revenue Account has a "Grand Total" column — we ALWAYS extract from Grand Total
- Hindi PDFs exist (e.g., As at June 30, 2025 has Hindi content)

---

## Quarter Label Convention (CALENDAR YEAR based)

The master CSV uses **calendar year + calendar quarter** labeling:
```
Q1 = January-March    → "As at March 31, YYYY"     → YYYY-Q1
Q2 = April-June       → "As at June 30, YYYY"      → YYYY-Q2
Q3 = July-September   → "As at September 30, YYYY" → YYYY-Q3
Q4 = October-December → "As at December 31, YYYY"  → YYYY-Q4
```

**Date-to-quarter mapping examples**:
- "As at March 31, 2026" → `2026-Q1`
- "As at June 30, 2025" → `2025-Q2`
- "As at September 30, 2025" → `2025-Q3`
- "As at December 31, 2025" → `2025-Q4`

**Indian FY to site mapping**:
- Site year "2025 - 2026" (FY 2025-26) contains: 2025-Q2, 2025-Q3, 2025-Q4, 2026-Q1

---

## Master CSV Structure

**File**: `Master_Data/Master_LICIPD_DATA.csv`

**Row 1**: Column codes (e.g., `LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.SHAREHOLDERS.Q`)
**Row 2**: Human-readable descriptions (e.g., `Balance Sheet L-3 Shareholders`)
**Row 3+**: Data rows with quarter label as index (e.g., `2022-Q2,1043687.34,...`)
**First column** (index): Quarter label (YYYY-QN)

**Total columns**: 56 data columns + 1 index column = 57
**Existing data**: 16 rows from 2022-Q2 through 2026-Q1

**Append rules**:
- New data appended as new row
- Quarter label checked for duplicates — skip if already exists
- NA for unavailable values
- Values stored as plain numbers (no Indian comma formatting)

---

## Hindi/Multilingual Support

PDFs and site text may appear in Hindi. Key considerations:
- The LIC site has a language toggle ("भाषा" button in header)
- Some quarterly reports are published in Hindi only (especially Q2/June)
- Revenue Account table headers remain in English structure but labels may be Hindi
- Balance Sheet has same table structure regardless of language
- The extractor must normalize Hindi numerals if encountered
- Hindi date conversion is handled by site JS but we need to handle in our scraper too

**Hindi-to-English label mappings needed** (based on observed PDFs):
- Table structure keywords: "LONG TERM" / "SHORT TERM" / "TOTAL" / "GRAND TOTAL" remain English typically
- Row labels for investments follow same structure
- Numbers use standard Arabic numerals even in Hindi PDFs

---

## Key Technical Decisions

### Extraction Library: PyMuPDF (fitz)
- Use `fitz` for ALL PDF table extraction (proven in OIRS_Runbook and AUSFEDGOVCF)
- Do NOT use pdfplumber (too slow) or camelot (overkill for these simple tables)
- `page.get_text("text")` for raw text, parse table structure from text layout
- OR `page.find_tables()` (fitz 1.23+) for structured table extraction

### Browser: Selenium Stealth (NOT Playwright)
- LIC site requires JS rendering and has bot detection
- Use `selenium-stealth` with `undetected-chromedriver`
- Chrome version detection: `winreg` on Windows, CLI fallback on Linux
- Must work with `headless=True` (Docker production)
- Human-like clicking delays between navigation steps

### Dynamic PDF Finding (NO hardcoded positions)
- PDF link text varies between dates (abbreviations, different naming)
- Must use fuzzy text matching on link text
- Search strategies:
  - Balance Sheet: look for "Balance Sheet" in link text
  - Investments PH: look for "Investments" AND ("Policyholders" OR "PHs")
  - Investments Linked: look for ("Investments" AND "Linked") OR "Assets held to cover linked"
  - Revenue Account: look for "Revenue Account" AND priority keyword

### Dynamic Table Extraction (NO hardcoded row/column positions)
- Find column headers dynamically: look for date pattern "As at [Month] [DD], [YYYY]"
- Pick the LATEST date column
- Find row labels by fuzzy matching against known label list
- Handle section headers (LONG TERM / SHORT TERM) as context markers
- Values: strip commas, handle parentheses as negative, handle "-" as zero/NA, handle "NIL" as NA

## META File Structure (56 rows)

All measures share these META attributes:
- FREQUENCY: Q (Quarterly)
- MULTIPLIER: 5 (Crore = 10^7)
- AGGREGATION_TYPE: END_OF_PERIOD
- UNIT_TYPE: FLOW
- DATA_TYPE: CURRENCY
- DATA_UNIT: INR
- SEASONALLY_ADJUSTED: NSA
- ANNUALIZED: False
- STATE: ACTIVE
- PROVIDER_MEASURE_URL: https://www.licindia.in/Bottom-Links/Public-disclosure
- PROVIDER: AfricaAI
- SOURCE: LIC
- SOURCE_DESCRIPTION: Life Insurance Corporation of India
- COUNTRY: IND
- DATASET: LICIPD

Each row differs only in CODE, CODE_MNEMONIC, and DESCRIPTION.

# LICIPD Runbook - Claude Working Context

## Project Status: ANALYSIS COMPLETE - Ready to build pipeline

---

## Project Summary

Automated quarterly extraction of LIC India (Life Insurance Corporation of India) public disclosure financial data from PDF reports published at https://www.licindia.in/Bottom-Links/Public-disclosure

Provider: AfricaAI | Dataset: LICIPD | Country: IND | Frequency: Quarterly
Currency: INR | Unit: Rs. Crore | Multiplier: 5 (10^7)

Pipeline: `main.py` -> `orchestrator.py` -> `scraper.py` -> `extractor.py` -> `file_generator.py`

56 data fields across 4 PDF report types. Master CSV append job (no duplicates).

---

## Pipeline Flow

```
python main.py
  |
  v
orchestrator.main()
  |
  |-- Step 1: scraper.download()
  |     - Selenium stealth browser (selenium-stealth + winreg/Linux fallback)
  |     - Navigate: Public Disclosure -> Year -> Date -> Find PDFs -> Download
  |     - Downloads 4 PDF categories (5 files total, Revenue has 2)
  |     - PDFs saved to downloads/<timestamp>/
  |
  |-- Step 2: extractor.extract(pdf_paths)
  |     - PyMuPDF (fitz) for all table extraction
  |     - Dynamic header/label detection (no hardcoded positions)
  |     - Handles English AND Hindi PDFs
  |     - Returns dict of {column_code: value} for all 56 fields
  |
  |-- Step 3: file_generator.generate(extracted_data)
  |     - Appends new quarter row to Master_Data/Master_LICIPD_DATA.csv
  |     - No duplicate quarters
  |     - Generates LICIPD_DATA output .xls
  |     - Generates LICIPD_META output .xls
  |     - Creates ZIP of outputs
  |     - Copies to output/latest/ and output/<timestamp>/
```

---

## Source Website Navigation (3-level deep)

### Level 1: Public Disclosure Main Page
- **URL**: https://www.licindia.in/Bottom-Links/Public-disclosure
- **Content**: List of financial years as clickable links (2005-2006 through 2025-2026)
- **HTML structure**: `<section id="maincontent">` -> `<ul>` -> `<li><a href="/web/guest/public-disclosure-YYYY-YY">`
- **Year link patterns** (INCONSISTENT - must handle all):
  - `/web/guest/public-disclosure-2025-26` (newer years use this pattern)
  - `/web/guest/public-disclosure-2024-25`
  - `/web/guest/public-disclosure-2023-241` (note: 241 not 24 - typo in site)
  - `/web/guest/2022-2023` (older years use plain format)
  - `/web/guest/2021-2022`
- **Config**: `TARGET_YEAR = None` means pick latest (first in list). Set to e.g. "2025 - 2026" to target specific year.

### Level 2: Year-Specific Date List
- **URL example**: https://www.licindia.in/web/guest/public-disclosure-2025-26
- **Content**: List of quarterly dates ("As at June 30, 2025", "As at September 30, 2025", etc.)
- **HTML structure**: `<section id="maincontent">` -> `<h1>Public Disclosure 2025-26</h1>` -> `<ul>` -> `<li><a href="/web/guest/as-at-month-dd-yyyy">`
- **Date link patterns**:
  - `/web/guest/as-at-june-30-20252` (note: trailing 2)
  - `/web/guest/as-at-september-30-2025`
  - `/web/guest/as-at-december-31-2025`
  - `/web/guest/as-at-march-31-2026`
- **Config**: `TARGET_DATE = None` means pick latest (last in list = most recent date). Can set specific date string.
- **IMPORTANT**: If PDFs are not yet available for latest date, fall back to previous date.

### Level 3: Report List Page (PDFs)
- **URL example**: https://www.licindia.in/web/guest/as-at-march-31-2026
- **Content**: Numbered table of PDF reports with download links
- **HTML structure**: `<table>` -> `<tr>` -> `<td><a href="/documents/20121/.../*.pdf/...">`
- **Reports are numbered** (e.g., 1-18+) but numbers change between dates
- **Must find PDFs DYNAMICALLY by text content**, not by position number

### PDF Viewer Behavior
- Clicking a PDF link opens LIC's built-in PDF viewer page (not direct download)
- URL pattern: `https://www.licindia.in/documents/20121/XXXXXXX/filename.pdf/uuid?t=timestamp`
- Must trigger download from viewer page (or intercept direct PDF URL from href)

---

## Four PDF Report Categories

### 1. Balance Sheet (L-3A / L-3)
- **Search text on report page**: "Balance Sheet" (look for L-3A or L-3)
- **Link text variations across dates**:
  - `L-3A- Balance Sheet as on 31.03.2026`
  - `L-3- Balance Sheet as at 30.06.2025`
  - `L-3A- Balance Sheet as at 31.12.2025`
- **PDF title**: "FORM L-3 (A)" or "BALANCE SHEET AS AT [DATE]"
- **Structure**: 2-page PDF, main data table on page 1
- **Columns**: "Schedule", "As at [Latest Date]", "As at [Previous Date]" -- always pick LATEST column
- **Values to extract** (3 fields from SOURCES OF FUNDS section):
  - `Shareholders` -> LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.SHAREHOLDERS.Q
  - `Policyholders` -> LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.POLICYHOLDERS.Q
  - `Asset Held to Cover Linked Liabilities` -> LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.ASSETSLINKEDLIABILITIES.Q
- **Page 2**: Contingent Liabilities table (NOT needed)
- **Amount unit**: Rs. Crore (shown in header)
- **Hindi consideration**: Label "Shareholders" may appear as Hindi equivalent

### 2. Investments Policyholders (L-13)
- **Search text on report page**: "Investments" + ("Policyholders" OR "PHs")
- **Link text variations**:

  - `L-13-Investments PHs as at 30.06.2025` (abbreviated!)
  - `L-13- Investments PHs as at 30.09.2025` (abbreviated!)

  5. Other than Approved Investments
  6. Other Current Assets (Net)

### 4. Revenue Account (L-1A / L-1)
- **THE MOST COMPLEX PDF** - requires special handling
- **Search text on report page**: "Revenue Account" + "period ended" (primary), "quarter ended" (fallback), "Half year" (last resort)
- **Priority order** (configurable via `REVENUE_ACCOUNT_PRIORITY`):
  1. "period ended" (default)
  2. "quarter ended"
  3. "Half year ended"
- **CRITICAL**: May find 2 PDFs with DIFFERENT dates (e.g., period ended 31.03.2025 AND period ended 31.03.2026). Must download BOTH and determine which is latest.
- **Latest determination**:
  1. First try: parse date from PDF filename (e.g., "31.03.2026" > "31.03.2025")
  2. Fallback: parse PDF content for "REVENUE ACCOUNT FOR THE PERIOD ENDED MARCH 31, 2026"
- **Link text variations**:
  - `L-1A- Revenue Account for the period ended 31.03.2026`
  - `L-1A- Revenue Account for the period ended 31.03.2025`
  - `L-1A- Revenue Account for the quarter ended 30.09.2024 (1)`
  - `L-1A- Revenue Account for the quarter ended 30.09.2025 (2)` (note parenthesized numbers)
  - `L-1- Revenue Account for the Half year ended 30.09.2025 (1)`
  - `L-1- Revenue Account for the period ended 30.06.2025`
  - `L-1- Revenue Account for the period ended 30.06.2024`

**PDF Structure**: Wide landscape table with many columns:
```
PARTICULARS | Schedule | LIFE | PENSION | HEALTH | UNI_TOTAL | ANNUITY | GROUP LINKED BUSINESS... | GRAND TOTAL
```
- **We extract from "GRAND TOTAL" column only** (last data column, rightmost)
- All values from the Grand Total row at the BOTTOM of the respective label section

**Values to extract** (10 fields, 3 are CALCULATED):

| # | PDF Label | Master Column Code | Notes |
|---|-----------|-------------------|-------|
| 1 | Premium (under "Premiums earned - net") | -- | Component a) |
| 2 | Reinsurance ceded | -- | Component b) |
| 3 | Reinsurance accepted | -- | Component c) |
| -- | **Premiums earned - net** | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.PREMIUMSNET.Q | **CALCULATED: a + b + c** (NOT in PDF directly) |
| 4 | Interest, Dividends & Rent - Gross | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.INTDIVINCOME.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 5 | Profit on sale/redemption of investments | -- | Component a) |
| 6 | (Loss on sale/redemption of investments) | -- | Component b), **parentheses = NEGATIVE** |
| -- | **Investment Gain/Loss On Sale/Redemption** | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.INVGAINLOSSSALE.Q | **CALCULATED: a + b** (b is negative if in parens) |
| 7 | Transfer/Gain on revaluation/change in fair value* | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.INVGAINLOSSREVAL.Q | Direct, may have asterisk |
| 8 | Other Income | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.OTHERINCOME.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 9 | TOTAL (A) | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.TOTALINCOME.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 10 | TOTAL (B) | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.OPERATINGEXP.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 11 | Benefits Paid (Net) | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.BENEFITSPAID.Q | Direct from PDF |
| 12 | Bonuses Paid | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.BONUSESPAID.Q | Direct - sometimes under "SURPLUS/DEFICIT" section |
| -- | **Net Income** | LICIPD.REVENUEACCOUNT.NETINCOME.Q | **CALCULATED: TOTAL(A) + TOTAL(B) + Benefits Paid + Bonuses Paid** |

**CRITICAL RULES for Revenue Account:**
- Values in parentheses `(1234.56)` = NEGATIVE: store as `-1234.56`
- "Reinsurance ceded" is typically negative (in parentheses)
- "(Loss on sale/redemption)" is typically negative (in parentheses)
- The Revenue Account has a "Grand Total" column -- we ALWAYS extract from Grand Total
- Hindi PDFs exist (e.g., As at June 30, 2025 has Hindi content)

---

## Quarter Label Convention (CALENDAR YEAR based)

The master CSV uses **calendar year + calendar quarter** labeling:
```
Q1 = January-March    -> "As at March 31, YYYY"     -> YYYY-Q1
Q2 = April-June       -> "As at June 30, YYYY"      -> YYYY-Q2
Q3 = July-September   -> "As at September 30, YYYY" -> YYYY-Q3
Q4 = October-December -> "As at December 31, YYYY"  -> YYYY-Q4
```

**Date-to-quarter mapping examples**:
- "As at March 31, 2026" -> `2026-Q1`
- "As at June 30, 2025" -> `2025-Q2`
- "As at September 30, 2025" -> `2025-Q3`
- "As at December 31, 2025" -> `2025-Q4`

**Indian FY to site mapping**:
- Site year "2025 - 2026" (FY 2025-26) contains: 2025-Q2, 2025-Q3, 2025-Q4, 2026-Q1

---

## Master CSV Structure

**File**: `Master_Data/Master_LICIPD_DATA.csv`

**Row 1**: Column codes (e.g., `LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.SHAREHOLDERS.Q`)
**Row 2**: Human-readable descriptions (e.g., `Balance Sheet L-3 Shareholders`)
**Row 3+**: Data rows with quarter label as index (e.g., `2022-Q2,1043687.34,...`)
**First column** (index): Quarter label (YYYY-QN)

**Total columns**: 56 data columns + 1 index column = 57
**Existing data**: 16 rows from 2022-Q2 through 2026-Q1

**Append rules**:
- New data appended as new row
- Quarter label checked for duplicates -- skip if already exists
- NA for unavailable values
- Values stored as plain numbers (no Indian comma formatting)

---

## Hindi/Multilingual Support

PDFs and site text may appear in Hindi. Key considerations:
- The LIC site has a language toggle in the header
- Some quarterly reports are published in Hindi only (especially Q2/June)
- Revenue Account table headers remain in English structure but labels may be Hindi
- Balance Sheet has same table structure regardless of language
- The extractor must normalize Hindi numerals if encountered
- Hindi date conversion is handled by site JS but we need to handle in our scraper too

---

## Key Technical Decisions

### Extraction Library: PyMuPDF (fitz)
- Use `fitz` for ALL PDF table extraction (proven in OIRS_Runbook and AUSFEDGOVCF)
- Do NOT use pdfplumber (too slow) or camelot (overkill for these simple tables)
- `page.get_text("text")` for raw text, parse table structure from text layout
- OR `page.find_tables()` (fitz 1.23+) for structured table extraction

### Browser: Selenium Stealth (NOT Playwright)
- LIC site requires JS rendering and has bot detection
- Use `selenium-stealth` with `undetected-chromedriver`
- Chrome version detection: `winreg` on Windows, CLI fallback on Linux
- Must work with `headless=True` (Docker production)
- Human-like clicking delays between navigation steps

### Dynamic PDF Finding (NO hardcoded positions)
- PDF link text varies between dates (abbreviations, different naming)
- Must use fuzzy text matching on link text
- Search strategies:
  - Balance Sheet: look for "Balance Sheet" in link text
  - Investments PH: look for "Investments" AND ("Policyholders" OR "PHs")
  - Investments Linked: look for ("Investments" AND "Linked") OR "Assets held to cover linked"
  - Revenue Account: look for "Revenue Account" AND priority keyword

### Dynamic Table Extraction (NO hardcoded row/column positions)
- Find column headers dynamically: look for date pattern "As at [Month] [DD], [YYYY]"
- Pick the LATEST date column
- Find row labels by fuzzy matching against known label list
- Handle section headers (LONG TERM / SHORT TERM) as context markers
- Values: strip commas, handle parentheses as negative, handle "-" as zero/NA, handle "NIL" as NA

## META File Structure (56 rows)

All measures share these META attributes:
- FREQUENCY: Q (Quarterly)
- MULTIPLIER: 5 (10^7)
- AGGREGATION_TYPE: END_OF_PERIOD
- UNIT_TYPE: FLOW
- DATA_TYPE: CURRENCY
- DATA_UNIT: INR
- SEASONALLY_ADJUSTED: NSA
- ANNUALIZED: False
- STATE: ACTIVE
- PROVIDER_MEASURE_URL: https://www.licindia.in/Bottom-Links/Public-disclosure
- PROVIDER: AfricaAI
- SOURCE: LIC
- SOURCE_DESCRIPTION: Life Insurance Corporation of India
- COUNTRY: IND
- DATASET: LICIPD

Each row differs only in CODE, CODE_MNEMONIC, and DESCRIPTION.

import os

# ── Paths ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
BASE_DIR     = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
DOWNLOAD_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, 'downloads')
OUTPUT_DIR   = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, 'output')
MASTER_DIR   = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, 'Master_Data')
MASTER_CSV   = os.path.join(MASTER_DIR, 'Master_LICIPD_DATA.csv')

# ── Source ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
BASE_URL = 'https://www.licindia.in/Bottom-Links/Public-disclosure'

# ── Browser ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
HEADLESS_MODE  = True
WAIT_TIMEOUT   = 60
PAGE_LOAD_WAIT = 5       # seconds to wait after page load
CLICK_DELAY    = (2, 4)  # random delay range (min, max) between clicks

# ── Target Selection (None = auto-detect latest) ─────────────────────────────
TARGET_YEAR = None        # e.g. "2025 - 2026" or None for latest
TARGET_DATE = None        # e.g. "As at March 31, 2026" or None for latest

# ── Revenue Account PDF Selection Priority ────────────────────────────────────
# Order of preference when multiple Revenue Account PDFs exist
# Options: "period ended", "quarter ended", "Half year ended"
REVENUE_ACCOUNT_PRIORITY = ["period ended", "quarter ended", "Half year ended"]

# ── Output ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
DATASET_NAME = 'LICIPD'
OUTPUT_DATA_PREFIX = 'LICIPD_DATA_'
OUTPUT_META_PREFIX = 'LICIPD_META_'
OUTPUT_ZIP_PREFIX  = 'LICIPD_'

# ── PDF Search Patterns (for finding links on report list page) ───────────────
# Each pattern is a list of keyword groups. ALL groups must match (AND logic).
# Within a group, any keyword matching is sufficient (OR logic).
PDF_SEARCH_PATTERNS = {
    'balance_sheet': {
        'keywords': [['Balance Sheet']],

"""
Test script for Balance Sheet (L-3A / L-3) PDF extraction using PyMuPDF (fitz).
Extracts: Shareholders, Policyholders, Asset Held to Cover Linked Liabilities
from the latest date column.
"""
import sys
import os
import re
import fitz  # PyMuPDF

sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
import config


def parse_value(text):
    """Parse a numeric value from PDF text. Handles Indian formatting, parentheses, NIL, dash."""
    if not text or not text.strip():
        return 'NA'
    text = text.strip()
    # Handle NIL
    if text.upper() == 'NIL':
        return 'NA'
    # Handle dash (no value)
    if text in ['-', '\u2013', '\u2014', '']:
        return 'NA'
    # Check for parentheses = negative
    is_negative = False
    if text.startswith('(') and text.endswith(')'):
        is_negative = True
        text = text[1:-1].strip()
    # Remove commas (Indian formatting: 1,50,740.33)
    text = text.replace(',', '')
    try:
        val = float(text)
        if is_negative:
            val = -val
        return val
    except ValueError:
        return 'NA'


def extract_balance_sheet(pdf_path):
    """Extract Balance Sheet values from PDF using fitz."""
    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"Extracting Balance Sheet from: {os.path.basename(pdf_path)}")
    print(f"{'='*70}")

    doc = fitz.open(pdf_path)
    page = doc[0]  # Balance sheet data is on page 1

    # Get raw text
    text = page.get_text("text")
    print(f"\nPage 1 raw text length: {len(text)} chars")

    # Try table extraction first (fitz built-in)
    tables = page.find_tables()
    print(f"Tables found on page 1: {len(tables.tables)}")

    results = {}
    date_detected = None

    if tables.tables:
        # Use the largest table (most rows)
        best_table = max(tables.tables, key=lambda t: len(t.extract()))
        rows = best_table.extract()

        print(f"\nBest table: {len(rows)} rows x {len(rows[0]) if rows else 0} cols")
        print("\n--- Raw table dump ---")
        for i, row in enumerate(rows):
            print(f"  Row {i:2d}: {row}")

        # Find the date columns - look for "As at" pattern
        header_row_idx = None
        date_col_indices = []
        for i, row in enumerate(rows):
            for j, cell in enumerate(row):
                if cell and re.search(r'as\s+at\s+\w+\s+\d{1,2},?\s*\d{4}', str(cell), re.IGNORECASE):
                    date_col_indices.append((j, cell.strip()))
                    if header_row_idx is None:
                        header_row_idx = i
                # Also check for "as on" pattern
                elif cell and re.search(r'as\s+on\s+\d{1,2}\.\d{2}\.\d{4}', str(cell), re.IGNORECASE):
                    date_col_indices.append((j, cell.strip()))
                    if header_row_idx is None:
                        header_row_idx = i

        print(f"\nDate columns found: {date_col_indices}")

        # Determine latest date column
        if date_col_indices:
            # Parse dates and find latest
            latest_col = None
            latest_date = None
            for col_idx, date_text in date_col_indices:
                # Extract date from text like "As at March 31, 2026" or "As at 31.03.2026"
                date_match = re.search(r'(\d{1,2})[./](\d{1,2})[./](\d{4})', date_text)
                if date_match:
                    day, month, year = int(date_match.group(1)), int(date_match.group(2)), int(date_match.group(3))
                else:
                    # Try "Month DD, YYYY" format
                    date_match = re.search(r'(\w+)\s+(\d{1,2}),?\s*(\d{4})', date_text)
                    if date_match:
                        month_name = date_match.group(1).lower()
                        day = int(date_match.group(2))
                        year = int(date_match.group(3))
                        month_map = {
                            'january': 1, 'february': 2, 'march': 3, 'april': 4,
                            'may': 5, 'june': 6, 'july': 7, 'august': 8,
                            'september': 9, 'october': 10, 'november': 11, 'december': 12,
                        }
                        month = month_map.get(month_name, 0)
                    else:
                        continue

                date_val = year * 10000 + month * 100 + day
                if latest_date is None or date_val > latest_date:
                    latest_date = date_val
                    latest_col = col_idx
                    date_detected = date_text

            print(f"Latest date column: index={latest_col}, date='{date_detected}'")

            if latest_col is not None:
                # Now scan rows for our target labels
                for i, row in enumerate(rows):
                    if i <= (header_row_idx or 0):
                        continue
                    # Check each cell for label match
                    label_cell = None
                    for cell in row:
                        if cell and cell.strip():
                            label_cell = cell.strip()
                            break
                    if not label_cell:
                        continue

                    label_lower = label_cell.lower().strip()
                    # Remove leading numbers and dots
                    label_lower = re.sub(r'^\d+\.?\s*', '', label_lower).strip()

                    for pattern, code in config.BALANCE_SHEET_LABELS.items():
                        if pattern in label_lower:
                            val_text = row[latest_col] if latest_col < len(row) else None
                            val = parse_value(val_text)
                            results[code] = val
                            print(f"  MATCH: '{label_cell}' -> {code} = {val}")
                            break

    # Fallback: text-based extraction if table extraction didn't get all fields
    if len(results) < 3:
        print("\nTable extraction incomplete, trying text-based fallback...")
        results_text = _extract_from_text(text)
        for k, v in results_text.items():
            if k not in results:
                results[k] = v
                print(f"  TEXT MATCH: {k} = {v}")

    doc.close()

    print(f"\n--- RESULTS ---")
    for code in ['LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.SHAREHOLDERS.Q',
                 'LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.POLICYHOLDERS.Q',
                 'LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.ASSETSLINKEDLIABILITIES.Q']:
        val = results.get(code, 'MISSING')
        print(f"  {code}: {val}")

    return results, date_detected


def _extract_from_text(text):
    """Fallback text-based extraction for Balance Sheet."""
    results = {}
    lines = text.split('\n')

    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        line_lower = line.lower().strip()
        for pattern, code in config.BALANCE_SHEET_LABELS.items():
            if pattern in line_lower and code not in results:
                # Look for numeric value in this line or nearby lines
                # Values are typically on the same line after the label
                numbers = re.findall(r'[\d,]+\.\d{2}', line)
                if numbers:
                    # Take the first number (latest column is typically first)
                    val = parse_value(numbers[0])
                    results[code] = val
                elif i + 1 < len(lines):
                    # Check next line
                    numbers = re.findall(r'[\d,]+\.\d{2}', lines[i + 1])
                    if numbers:
                        val = parse_value(numbers[0])
                        results[code] = val
    return results


def date_to_quarter(date_text):
    """Convert date text to quarter label. E.g. 'As at March 31, 2026' -> '2026-Q1'"""
    if not date_text:
        return None
    # Try DD.MM.YYYY
    m = re.search(r'(\d{1,2})[./](\d{1,2})[./](\d{4})', date_text)
    if m:
        month = int(m.group(2))
        year = int(m.group(3))
    else:
        # Try "Month DD, YYYY"
        m = re.search(r'(\w+)\s+(\d{1,2}),?\s*(\d{4})', date_text)
        if m:
            month_map = {
                'january': 1, 'february': 2, 'march': 3, 'april': 4,
                'may': 5, 'june': 6, 'july': 7, 'august': 8,
                'september': 9, 'october': 10, 'november': 11, 'december': 12,
            }
            month = month_map.get(m.group(1).lower(), 0)
            year = int(m.group(3))
        else:
            return None

    quarter = config.MONTH_TO_QUARTER.get(month)
    if quarter:
        return f"{year}-{quarter}"
    return None

"""
Test script for Balance Sheet (L-3A / L-3) PDF extraction using PyMuPDF (fitz).
Extracts: Shareholders, Policyholders, Asset Held to Cover Linked Liabilities
from the latest date column.
"""
import sys
import os
import re
import io
import fitz  # PyMuPDF

sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
import config

# Force UTF-8 output on Windows
if sys.platform == 'win32':
    sys.stdout = io.TextIOWrapper(sys.stdout.buffer, encoding='utf-8', errors='replace')


MONTH_NAME_MAP = {
    'january': 1, 'jan': 1, 'jan.': 1,
    'february': 2, 'feb': 2, 'feb.': 2,
    'march': 3, 'mar': 3, 'mar.': 3,
    'april': 4, 'apr': 4, 'apr.': 4,
    'may': 5,
    'june': 6, 'jun': 6, 'jun.': 6,
    'july': 7, 'jul': 7, 'jul.': 7,
    'august': 8, 'aug': 8, 'aug.': 8,
    'september': 9, 'sept': 9, 'sept.': 9, 'sep': 9, 'sep.': 9,
    'october': 10, 'oct': 10, 'oct.': 10,
    'november': 11, 'nov': 11, 'nov.': 11,
    'december': 12, 'dec': 12, 'dec.': 12,
}

# Schedule Reference -> Column Code mapping (most reliable for Balance Sheet)
SCHEDULE_REF_MAP = {
    'L-12': 'LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.SHAREHOLDERS.Q',
    'L-13': 'LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.POLICYHOLDERS.Q',
    'L-14': 'LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.ASSETSLINKEDLIABILITIES.Q',
}


def parse_value(text):
    """Parse a numeric value from PDF text. Handles Indian formatting, parentheses, NIL, dash."""
    if not text or not text.strip():
        return 'NA'
    text = text.strip()
    if text.upper() == 'NIL':
        return 'NA'
    if text in ['-', '\u2013', '\u2014', '']:
        return 'NA'
    is_negative = False
    if text.startswith('(') and text.endswith(')'):
        is_negative = True
        text = text[1:-1].strip()
    text = text.replace(',', '')
    try:
        val = float(text)
        if is_negative:
            val = -val
        return val
    except ValueError:
        return 'NA'


def parse_date_from_text(text):
    """Parse date from header text. Returns (day, month, year) or None.
    Handles: 'As at March 31, 2026', 'As at Sept. 30, 2025', 'As at 31.12.2025'
    """
    if not text:
        return None
    text = text.replace('\n', ' ').strip()

    # Try DD.MM.YYYY or DD/MM/YYYY
    m = re.search(r'(\d{1,2})[./](\d{1,2})[./](\d{4})', text)
    if m:
        return int(m.group(1)), int(m.group(2)), int(m.group(3))

    # Try "Month DD, YYYY" or "Month. DD, YYYY" (handles abbreviated months)
    m = re.search(r'(\w+\.?)\s+(\d{1,2}),?\s*(\d{4})', text)
    if m:
        month_str = m.group(1).lower()
        month = MONTH_NAME_MAP.get(month_str, 0)
        if month > 0:
            return int(m.group(2)), month, int(m.group(3))

    return None


def detect_date_columns(rows):
    """Find date columns in table header rows. Returns list of (col_index, date_text, date_value)."""
    date_cols = []
    for i, row in enumerate(rows[:5]):  # Only check first 5 rows for headers
        for j, cell in enumerate(row):
            if not cell:
                continue
            cell_clean = cell.replace('\n', ' ').strip()
            # Look for "As at" or "As on" prefix with a date
            if re.search(r'as\s+(at|on)\s+', cell_clean, re.IGNORECASE):
                parsed = parse_date_from_text(cell_clean)
                if parsed:
                    day, month, year = parsed
                    date_val = year * 10000 + month * 100 + day
                    date_cols.append((j, cell_clean, date_val))
    return date_cols


def extract_balance_sheet(pdf_path):
    """Extract Balance Sheet values from PDF using fitz."""
    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"Extracting Balance Sheet from: {os.path.basename(pdf_path)}")
    print(f"{'='*70}")

    doc = fitz.open(pdf_path)
    page = doc[0]

    tables = page.find_tables()
    print(f"Tables found on page 1: {len(tables.tables)}")

    results = {}
    date_detected = None

    if not tables.tables:
        print("ERROR: No tables found on page 1!")
        doc.close()
        return results, date_detected

    best_table = max(tables.tables, key=lambda t: len(t.extract()))
    rows = best_table.extract()
    print(f"Best table: {len(rows)} rows x {len(rows[0]) if rows else 0} cols")

    # Detect date columns
    date_cols = detect_date_columns(rows)
    print(f"Date columns detected: {[(c[0], c[1]) for c in date_cols]}")

    if not date_cols:
        print("ERROR: No date columns detected!")
        doc.close()
        return results, date_detected

    # Pick latest date column
    latest = max(date_cols, key=lambda x: x[2])
    latest_col_idx = latest[0]
    date_detected = latest[1]
    print(f"Using latest: col={latest_col_idx}, date='{date_detected}'")

    # Find APPLICATION OF FUNDS section start
    app_of_funds_row = None
    for i, row in enumerate(rows):
        for cell in row:
            if cell and 'application of funds' in cell.lower():
                app_of_funds_row = i
                break
        if app_of_funds_row is not None:
            break

    search_start = app_of_funds_row if app_of_funds_row is not None else 0
    print(f"APPLICATION OF FUNDS starts at row {search_start}")

    # Primary method: Match by Schedule Reference (L-12, L-13, L-14)
    # The Schedule Ref column is typically column index 2
    schedule_col = None
    for j, cell in enumerate(rows[0]):
        if cell and 'schedule' in cell.lower():
            schedule_col = j
            break

    if schedule_col is not None:
        print(f"Schedule reference column: {schedule_col}")
        for i, row in enumerate(rows):
            if i <= search_start:
                continue
            if schedule_col < len(row) and row[schedule_col]:
                ref = row[schedule_col].strip()
                for sched_ref, code in SCHEDULE_REF_MAP.items():
                    if sched_ref in ref:
                        val_text = row[latest_col_idx] if latest_col_idx < len(row) else None
                        val = parse_value(val_text)
                        results[code] = val
                        label = row[1].strip() if len(row) > 1 and row[1] else '?'
                        print(f"  MATCH [{sched_ref}]: '{label}' = {val}")
                        break

    # Fallback: text-based label matching in APPLICATION OF FUNDS section
    if len(results) < 3:
        print(f"\nSchedule ref got {len(results)}/3, trying label fallback...")
        for i, row in enumerate(rows):
            if i <= search_start:
                continue
            label_cell = None
            for cell in row:
                if cell and cell.strip():
                    label_cell = cell.strip()
                    break
            if not label_cell:
                continue

            label_lower = label_cell.lower().strip()
            # Clean up: remove unicode chars, trailing colons, leading numbers
            label_lower = re.sub(r'[^\x00-\x7f]', '', label_lower).strip()
            label_lower = re.sub(r'^\d+\.?\s*', '', label_lower).strip()
            label_lower = label_lower.rstrip(':').strip()

            for pattern, code in config.BALANCE_SHEET_LABELS.items():
                if code not in results and pattern in label_lower:
                    val_text = row[latest_col_idx] if latest_col_idx < len(row) else None
                    val = parse_value(val_text)
                    if val != 'NA':  # Only accept if we got a real value
                        results[code] = val
                        print(f"  LABEL MATCH: '{label_cell}' -> {code} = {val}")
                    break

    doc.close()

    print(f"\n--- RESULTS ---")
    expected_codes = [
        'LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.SHAREHOLDERS.Q',
        'LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.POLICYHOLDERS.Q',
        'LICIPD.BALANCESHEET.ASSETSLINKEDLIABILITIES.Q',
    ]
    for code in expected_codes:
        val = results.get(code, 'MISSING')
        print(f"  {code}: {val}")

    return results, date_detected


def date_to_quarter(date_text):
    """Convert date text to quarter label. E.g. 'As at March 31, 2026' -> '2026-Q1'"""
    if not date_text:
        return None
    parsed = parse_date_from_text(date_text)
    if not parsed:
        return None
    _, month, year = parsed
    quarter = config.MONTH_TO_QUARTER.get(month)
    if quarter:
        return f"{year}-{quarter}"
    return None

                match = True
                for code, exp_val in expected.items():
                    got = results.get(code, 'MISSING')
                    if isinstance(got, float) and abs(got - exp_val) < 0.01:
                        print(f"  VERIFY OK: {code} = {got} (expected {exp_val})")
                    else:
                        print(f"  VERIFY FAIL: {code} = {got} (expected {exp_val})")
                        match = False
                if not match:
                    all_pass = False
            else:
                print(f"  OK: All 3 fields extracted (no expected values to verify)")

    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"Overall: {'ALL PASS' if all_pass else 'SOME FAILURES'}")

"""
Test script for Investments Policyholders (L-13) PDF extraction using PyMuPDF (fitz).
Extracts 28 fields: 17 LONG TERM + 11 SHORT TERM from the latest date column.
"""
import sys
import os
import re
import io
import fitz

sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
import config
from test_balance_sheet import parse_value, parse_date_from_text, detect_date_columns, date_to_quarter, MONTH_NAME_MAP

if sys.platform == 'win32':
    sys.stdout = io.TextIOWrapper(sys.stdout.buffer, encoding='utf-8', errors='replace')


def clean_label(text):
    """Clean a PDF row label for matching. Strips prefixes, numbering, sub-item markers."""
    if not text:
        return ''
    t = text.strip()
    # Remove leading row numbers: "1", "2", etc.
    t = re.sub(r'^\d+\.?\s*', '', t).strip()
    # Remove sub-item prefixes: "(a)", "(aa)", "(b)", "(bb)", "(c)", "(d)", "(e)", "(f)", "(g)"
    t = re.sub(r'^\([a-z]+\)\s*', '', t).strip()
    # Remove trailing colons and dashes: "Other Securities:-" -> "Other Securities"
    t = re.sub(r'[:\-]+$', '', t).strip()
    # Collapse whitespace
    t = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', t)
    return t.lower()


def extract_investments_ph(pdf_path):
    """Extract Investments Policyholders values from L-13 PDF."""
    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"Extracting L-13 from: {os.path.basename(pdf_path)}")
    print(f"{'='*70}")

    doc = fitz.open(pdf_path)
    page = doc[0]
    tables = page.find_tables()

    if not tables.tables:
        print("ERROR: No tables found!")
        doc.close()
        return {}, None

    best_table = max(tables.tables, key=lambda t: len(t.extract()))
    rows = best_table.extract()
    print(f"Table: {len(rows)} rows x {len(rows[0]) if rows else 0} cols")

    # Detect date columns
    date_cols = detect_date_columns(rows)
    print(f"Date columns: {[(c[0], c[1]) for c in date_cols]}")

    if not date_cols:
        print("ERROR: No date columns detected!")
        doc.close()
        return {}, None

    latest = max(date_cols, key=lambda x: x[2])
    latest_col = latest[0]
    date_detected = latest[1]
    print(f"Using latest: col={latest_col}, date='{date_detected}'")

    results = {}
    section = None  # 'long_term' or 'short_term'

    for i, row in enumerate(rows):
        # Get label from the widest text cell (skip row number column)
        label_text = ''
        for cell in row:
            if cell and len(str(cell).strip()) > len(label_text):
                label_text = str(cell).strip()

        # Also check column 1 specifically (main label column)
        if len(row) > 1 and row[1]:
            label_col1 = row[1].strip()
        else:
            label_col1 = ''

        # Use the longer of the two
        raw_label = label_col1 if len(label_col1) >= len(label_text) else label_text

        # Detect section markers
        raw_lower = raw_label.lower().replace('\n', ' ')
        if 'long term investment' in raw_lower:
            section = 'long_term'
            print(f"  [Section: LONG TERM] row {i}")
            continue
        elif 'short term investment' in raw_lower:
            section = 'short_term'
            print(f"  [Section: SHORT TERM] row {i}")
            continue

        if section is None:
            continue

        # Clean the label for matching
        cleaned = clean_label(raw_label)
        if not cleaned:
            continue

        # Get value from latest column
        val_text = row[latest_col] if latest_col < len(row) else None
        val = parse_value(val_text)

        # Try to match against config labels
        key = (section, cleaned)
        code = config.INVPHS_LABELS.get(key)

        if code is None:
            # Try partial matching for labels that might differ slightly
            for config_key, config_code in config.INVPHS_LABELS.items():
                if config_key[0] == section and config_key[1] in cleaned:
                    code = config_code
                    break
                # Also try if cleaned is contained in config key
                if config_key[0] == section and cleaned in config_key[1] and len(cleaned) > 3:
                    code = config_code
                    break

        if code and code not in results:
            results[code] = val
            print(f"  MATCH: [{section}] '{raw_label}' -> {code.split('.')[-2]} = {val}")

    doc.close()

    # Print summary
    print(f"\n--- RESULTS ({len(results)}/28 fields) ---")
    expected_lt = [c for c in config.COLUMN_CODES if 'INVPHS.LONGTERM' in c]
    expected_st = [c for c in config.COLUMN_CODES if 'INVPHS.SHORTTERM' in c]

    print("  LONG TERM:")
    for code in expected_lt:
        val = results.get(code, 'NA')
        short = code.split('.')[-2]
        print(f"    {short}: {val}")

    print("  SHORT TERM:")
    for code in expected_st:
        val = results.get(code, 'NA')
        short = code.split('.')[-2]
        print(f"    {short}: {val}")

    return results, date_detected


# Expected values from master CSV for verification
EXPECTED_VALUES = {
    '2026-Q1': {
        'LICIPD.INVPHS.LONGTERM.GOVTSECS.Q': 3198707.72,

}


if __name__ == '__main__':
    test_pdfs = []

    march = os.path.join(config.BASE_DIR, 'Project_information',

    if os.path.exists(dec):
        test_pdfs.append(('December 2025', dec))

    sep = os.path.join(config.BASE_DIR, 'Project_information', 'samplepdfs',
                       'As at September 30, 2025',

    if os.path.exists(sep):
        test_pdfs.append(('September 2025', sep))

    jun = os.path.join(config.BASE_DIR, 'Project_information', 'samplepdfs',
                       'As at June 30, 2025',

    if os.path.exists(jun):
        test_pdfs.append(('June 2025', jun))

    if not test_pdfs:
        print("No test PDFs found!")
        sys.exit(1)

    print(f"Found {len(test_pdfs)} test PDFs")
    all_pass = True

    for label, pdf_path in test_pdfs:
        print(f"\n{'#'*70}")
        print(f"# Testing: {label}")
        print(f"{'#'*70}")
        results, date_text = extract_investments_ph(pdf_path)
        quarter = date_to_quarter(date_text)
        print(f"\nQuarter: {quarter}, Fields extracted: {len(results)}")

        if quarter and quarter in EXPECTED_VALUES:
            expected = EXPECTED_VALUES[quarter]
            for code, exp_val in expected.items():
                got = results.get(code, 'MISSING')
                if isinstance(got, (int, float)) and abs(got - exp_val) < 0.01:
                    pass  # OK
                else:
                    print(f"  VERIFY FAIL: {code.split('.')[-2]} = {got} (expected {exp_val})")
                    all_pass = False
            print(f"  Verified {len(expected)} values against master CSV")
        else:
            if len(results) < 15:
                print(f"  WARNING: Only {len(results)} fields extracted")
                all_pass = False

    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"Overall: {'ALL PASS' if all_pass else 'SOME FAILURES'}")
    print(f"{'='*70}")

Traceback (most recent call last):
  File "D:\Projects\SIMBA-RUNBOOKS\LICIPD_Runbook\test_investments_ph.py", line 207, in <module>
    print(f"Found {len(test_pdfs)} test PDFs")
ValueError: I/O operation on closed file.
The issue is that the import of test_balance_sheet is running that module's if __name__ == '__main__' block... wait no, that shouldn't happen since it's imported as a module. The issue might be that test_balance_sheet.py sets sys.stdout to a new TextIOWrapper, and when we also set it in this file, there might be a conflict.

Wait, actually the issue is: test_balance_sheet.py has this code at module level (not in __main__):


if sys.platform == 'win32':
    sys.stdout = io.TextIOWrapper(sys.stdout.buffer, encoding='utf-8', errors='replace')
When we import test_balance_sheet, this code runs and replaces sys.stdout. Then when we do it again in test_investments_ph.py, we're wrapping the already-wrapped stdout. The buffer from the first wrapper might get closed when the second wrapper takes over.

The fix is to move that stdout configuration into the __name__ == '__main__' block in the balance sheet module so it only runs when that file is executed directly, not when it's imported.

The stdout wrapping is conflicting between imports. Let me fix the approach - move stdout wrapping to a shared utility.

Now I can see the Hindi L-13 table. Key Hindi terms:

Row 2: 'लंबी अविध के िनवेश' = "Long term investments" (Hindi: लंबी अवधि के निवेश)

Row 18: 'लघु अविध के िनवेश' = "Short term investments" (Hindi: लघु अवधि के निवेश)

Row 33: 'कुल' = "Total"

Row 6: '(aa) इिƓटी' = "(aa) Equity"

Row 7: '(bb) वरीयता' = "(bb) Preference"

The pattern here uses "लंबी अविध" or "लंबी अवधि" for long-term categories and "लघु अविध" or "लघु अवधि" for short-term ones.

Since the Hindi labels are completely different from the English text, I need to rely on positional matching within each section rather than text comparison. The row structure is consistent across languages—government securities always come first, followed by approved securities, then the shares subsections with equity and preference, mutual funds, derivatives, debentures, and other securities in the same order every time.

But positional matching alone is risky since rows can vary. A better approach is to use the structural prefixes as anchors—the numbered items (1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6) and sub-item markers like (a), (aa), (bb), (b), (c), (d), (e), (f), (g) appear consistently in the first column regardless of language, so I can use these as reliable identifiers to map the data correctly. Continuing with the remaining long-term categories and their mappings, then noticing the Hindi text uses the same structural prefixes like (a), (aa), (bb), (b), (d), (e) for the sub-items, which means the pattern should be consistent across both language versions. Building the structural mapping... Mapping more investment categories... I'm noticing some gaps in the mapping—there are a few fields from the config that don't appear in the recent PDFs, like deposits with the Social Security Fund and the initial UTI contribution. For the long-term "Other Securities & Bonds" category, there's a structural quirk where the header row is empty but the actual data sits in the next row, and this pattern differs between the English and Hindi versions.

My approach is to use row numbers and sub-item prefixes as the primary matching mechanism, then add special handling for cases like the (e) header where I need to check both the header row and the following rows for the actual value, plus account for the "TOTAL"/"कुल" markers in the short-term section and add Hindi section identifiers.

Rewriting the extraction function...

Now I can see the full Hindi structure. The sub-item prefixes (aa), (bb), (b), (d), etc. are English even in Hindi PDFs. I'll use structural matching (row numbers + sub-item prefixes) as the primary strategy -- this works for both languages.

dont hard code possition ensure the code is as context aware as possible and highly dynamic some times the lables can iter change possitions then what
You're absolutely right. No hardcoded positions -- the extraction must be fully dynamic using structural markers that are language-agnostic. The sub-item prefixes (aa), (bb), (b), (d) etc. are always in English even in Hindi PDFs, and row numbers in column 0 (1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6) are always present. Combined with section detection, this gives us a robust language-independent matching system.

   - Hindi/English bilingual PDF handling - PDFs can be in either language
   - Indian number formatting (XX,XX,XXX.XX lakh/crore grouping) -> plain float
   - Parenthesized values = negative numbers: `(1234.56)` -> `-1234.56`
   - Calendar year quarter labeling: Q1=March, Q2=June, Q3=Sept, Q4=Dec
   - Dynamic date detection handling abbreviated months ("Sept.") and Hindi months ("जून")
   - Structural matching using language-agnostic markers (row numbers, sub-item prefixes like (aa), (bb))
   - Revenue Account calculated fields (Premiums net, Investment Gain/Loss, Net Income)
   - Master CSV append-only with duplicate quarter prevention
   - Cross-platform paths with os.path.join() (Windows dev, Docker Linux prod)

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **UnicodeEncodeError on Windows console (cp1252)**: PDF text contains special chars. Fixed with `_ensure_utf8_stdout()` wrapping sys.stdout in TextIOWrapper with UTF-8 encoding.
   - **Date detection failed for abbreviated months**: "As at Sept. 30, 2025" didn't match regex. Fixed by adding full MONTH_NAME_MAP with all abbreviations (sept, sept., sep, sep., etc.).
   - **Date detection failed for Hindi dates**: "30 जून, 2025 तक" not detected. Fixed by adding Hindi month names to MONTH_NAME_MAP and Hindi date format parsing ("DD [Hindi month], YYYY") in parse_date_from_text().
   - **Balance Sheet false matches on section headers**: "SHAREHOLDERS' FUNDS:" (Sources section) matched before "Shareholders'" (Application section). Fixed by using Schedule Reference matching (L-12/L-13/L-14) and restricting search to APPLICATION OF FUNDS section.
   - **Hindi Balance Sheet schedule refs**: "एल-12" / "एल 12" not matching "L-12". Fixed by normalizing Hindi "एल" to "L" and "एल 12" -> "L-12".
   - **L-13 label cell overridden by value cell**: "(aa) Equity" (11 chars) was replaced by "12,68,775.38" (12 chars) in "longest text cell" logic. Fixed by always using column 1 as label column.
   - **L-13 "Other Securities:-" header matched before "Other Securities & Bonds" data row**: Header had NA value, blocked the real data row. Fixed by allowing value override: if code exists with NA and new match has non-NA value, replace it.
   - **L-13 TOTAL not captured**: Same "longest text cell" bug - "TOTAL" (5 chars) overridden by value (12 chars). Fixed by same column 1 approach.
   - **stdout wrapper conflict between imported modules**: test_balance_sheet.py set sys.stdout at module level, conflicting when imported by test_investments_ph.py. Fixed by moving to `_ensure_utf8_stdout()` function called only in `__main__`.
   - **User feedback - Hindi assumption**: User explicitly said "you need to always remember any of the pdfs can be in hindi so always account for that never assume". This means EVERY extraction function must handle Hindi from the start.
   - **User feedback - No hardcoded positions**: User said "dont hard code position ensure the code is as context aware as possible and highly dynamic some times the labels can change positions then what". This means using structural markers (row numbers, sub-item prefixes) rather than positional assumptions.

5. Problem Solving:
   - Balance Sheet extraction: SOLVED - 4/4 ALL PASS using Schedule Reference matching + section filtering
   - L-13 Investments Policyholders: PARTIALLY SOLVED - English PDFs work after fixes, but Hindi PDF still fails because:
     1. Section markers are Hindi text not recognized
     2. Even after section fix, English label matching won't work on Hindi labels
     3. Need structural matching using row numbers (col 0: 1,2,3,4,5,6) and sub-item prefixes ((aa),(bb),(b),(d),(e),(f),(g),(i)) which are language-agnostic
   - Key architectural insight discovered: Sub-item prefixes like (aa), (bb), (b), (d) are ALWAYS English even in Hindi PDFs. Row numbers in column 0 are always Arabic numerals. These provide language-independent structural anchors.

   **Strategy 2 (verification/fallback)**: English label text matching against config.INVPHS_LABELS
